              <div class="preview-text spaced spaced-top story-preview spaced-md hddn-mble hddn-dktp hddn-tbl hddn-mble four-column-item" data-pb-field="description.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here.">
               World War II veteran and 106-year-old retired U.S. Navy pilot Robbie Roberts gets a tour of the MH-60R Seahawk helicopter during a ceremony at Orlando Executive Airport, Thursday, March 11, 2021. Roberts is the oldest living Naval helicopter pilot and was presented with the Naval Helicopter Association "Lifetime Achievement Award" by several U.S. Navy Florida-based flight crews, including pilots from the HSM-40 Airwolves maritime strike force from Naval Station Mayport, Jacksonville. The Airwolves flew two Seahawks from Mayport to Orlando for the ceremony, Thursday morning. Roberts will celebrate his 107th birthday on April 17. (Joe Burbank/Orlando Sentinel)
